creations-chat 2021-06-15 06:56:13 A close-in weapon system (CIWS /ÀàsiÀêw…™z/ SEE-wiz)[1] is a point-defense weapon system for detecting and destroying short-range incoming missiles and enemy aircraft which have penetrated the outer defenses, typically mounted shipboard in a naval capacity. Nearly all classes of larger modern warships are equipped with some kind of CIWS device.

There are two types of CIWS systems. A gun-based CIWS usually consists of a combination of radars, computers, and rapid-firing multiple-barrel rotary cannons placed on a rotating turret. Missile-based CIWSs use either infra-red, passive radar/ESM, or semi-active radar terminal guidance to guide missiles to the targeted enemy aircraft or other threats. In some cases, CIWS are used on land to protect military bases. In this case, the CIWS can also protect the base from shell and rocket fire.

creations-chat 2022-01-23 00:43:42 Off topic, but a quick guide to your/you're

You're is short for **you are**. It doesn't make sense in "I love you're build" because it means "I love you are build." It would make sense in " You're such a good builder!"

Your is used for when you are referring to another person's thing. "Your build is great!" "Can I have a look at your plane?"

creations-chat 2022-03-30 12:38:56 a quick guide to your/you're

You're is short for you are. It doesn't make sense in "I love you're build" because it means "I love you are build."

Your is used for when you are referring to another person's thing. "Your build is great!" "Can I have a look at your plane?"
creations-chat 2022-03-30 12:40:59 I did actually make this myself

You and anyone else are free to use it to help people fix their grammar

creations-chat 2022-05-10 21:22:50 a quick guide to your/you're

You're is short for you are. It doesn't make sense in "I love you're build" because it means "I love you are build."

Your is used for when you are referring to another person's thing. "Your build is great!" "Can I have a look at your plane?"

Free use. Help people better their grammar.

help 2022-07-18 05:15:23 1. Camera locking is a way of angle locking that doesn't require motors

It's good for parts of a build that would otherwise be overcomplicated by angled components

Camera lock welds to the pilot seat, so you can't connect it with a motorlock tower

2. Piston lock is a way of fine tuning the position of a block or component so it can fill a space effectively

This is good for highly technically complex builds that have many different shapes 

It can be glitchy

Usually these two are used in tandem with motorlocking (especially piston  lock) to enhance the effect motorlocking components onto a build has

creations-chat 2022-07-31 09:37:46 a quick guide to your/you're

You're is short for you are. It doesn't make sense in "I love you're build" because it means "I love you are build."

Your is used for when you are referring to another person's thing. "Your build is great!" "Can I have a look at your plane?"

creations-chat 2022-09-02 15:09:59 u don't let go of any key when u want to stop the motor movement, you instead press and hold down both the key u used to move it and the key that counteracts the movement

Forwards = F, Backwards = R

Hold down F to move to desired location

WITHOUT LETTING GO OF F press and hold down R and hold both keys for 5 seconds

Timing is important

help 2022-10-06 14:06:32 Workaround for Bugged Signs (for the uninformed)

**To type on the sign** click on the sign / text with the config tool and enter your text

***NOTE*** you **CANNOT** colour or change its material first, you **MUST ALWAYS DO IT AFTER YOU ADD YOUR TEXT** otherwise it will **BUG**

**To colour the sign or text block** Click on the **back** with your paint colour of choice. **To change the material of the sign** is the same as the above process but for material

**You can also drag across the side of a sign block to colour / change the material of said block. It works for colouring the text on a sign block.**

creations-chat 2022-10-08 08:05:44 hello Mortified_AWACS

Full tutorial

Go to www.photopea.com (you can use others but this one is the most convenient)

1. Press "New Project"

2. Set resolution to desired one (not required) and then press "Create"

3. Open an image of your blueprint (use "edit" --> "transform" --> "scale" and resize it

4. Create a new layer and place it on top of the layer you have your blueprint on (Go to "Layer" --> "New" --> "Layer)

Your new layer should be visible on the right hand side of the screen in the layers panel

5. Select your new layer (name is default "Layer 1", change opacity to 50% (this setting is visible directly above your layers)

6. Insert an image of your plane on the new layer and go "edit" --> "transform" --> "scale" to resize it and "edit" --> "transform" --> "rotate" to rotate it

7. Enjoy

Note: do not under any circumstance use "free transform"  because you might mess up the scale of your build
